# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

The getDSQueryEndpoint() handler detects feature flags to either route to the legacy path or the new query service API.\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go** - Kubernetes-style REST API layer implementing the K8s API server pattern. The queryREST struct implements the Connect() method which returns an HTTP handler that processes POST requests to execute queries. This is the primary entry point for the new query service.\\n\\n## 2. Query Request Handler and Dispatch\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go** - The handleQuery() function processes incoming QueryDataRequest objects, extracts headers, and routes to the appropriate handler. The prepareQuery() function normalizes datasource references and builds the MetricRequest used by the legacy query service. The handlePreparedQuery() function invokes the legacy query service.\\n\\n**pkg/services/query/query.go** - The ServiceImpl implements the core query execution logic. Key methods:\\n- queryData() - Routes queries based on whether they contain expressions or target single/multiple datasources\\n- handleQuerySingleDatasource() - For single datasource queries, creates a backend.QueryDataRequest and dispatches to either the legacy plugin client (single-tenant) or the query-service client (multi-tenant) via ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest()\\n- handleExpressions() - For expression queries, delegates to the expression service's TransformData()\\n- executeConcurrentQueries() - Handles multiple datasource queries concurrently and aggregates responses\\n\\n## 3. Plugin Backend Query Dispatch\\n\\n**pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go** - The Service.QueryData() method looks up the plugin from the registry and invokes its QueryData handler. It handles error wrapping, request cancellation, and ensures frame RefIDs are set from response RefIDs.\\n\\n**pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go** - Core plugin implementation that wraps backend plugin handlers and invokes them with proper Grafana config context.\\n\\n**pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/query.go** - The QueryDataHandler() processes query requests in the aggregator layer (for multi-tenant deployments). It validates datasource references, obtains plugin context, and dispatches to the plugin client.\\n\\n**pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/handler.go** - The PluginHandler routes requests to appropriate service handlers based on the aggregation service specification. For QueryServiceType, it routes to the QueryDataHandler().\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/datasource/sub_query.go** - Sub-resource query handler for direct datasource querying. The Connect() method returns an HTTP handler that binds the QueryDataRequest, extracts queries, and dispatches to the plugin client.\\n\\n## 4. Expression and Query Transformation\\n\\n**pkg/expr/service.go** - The Service.TransformData() method processes expression pipelines. It executes the expression graph using the datasource clients to fetch data and transform it according to the expression configuration.\\n\\n**pkg/expr/query_convert.go** - ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest() converts backend.QueryDataRequest to the K8s-style data.QueryDataRequest format used by the query-service client. This enables single datasource queries in multi-tenant scenarios.\\n\\n## 5. Response Transformation and Marshaling\\n\\n**pkg/apis/datasource/v0alpha1/query.go** - Defines the QueryDataResponse wrapper type that embeds backend.QueryDataResponse and adds Kubernetes metadata. The GetResponseCode() helper function determines the appropriate HTTP status code based on response content.\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go** - In the Connect() method's handler, the responder.Object() calls wrap the backend.QueryDataResponse in a query.QueryDataResponse before serialization. Error handling converts errors to appropriate error responses with proper status codes and error sources.\\n\\n**pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/** - Middleware chain that wraps the plugin client:\\n- caching_middleware.go - Caches query results when applicable\\n- httpclient_middleware.go - Sets HTTP headers on plugin requests\\n- metrics_middleware.go - Records request metrics\\n- tracing_middleware.go - Adds distributed tracing spans\\n\\nThese middleware components intercept QueryData calls to add cross-cutting concerns before dispatching to the underlying plugin implementation.\\n\\n## Complete Query Path Chain\\n\\n1. HTTP request arrives at getDSQueryEndpoint() or queryREST.Connect()\\n2. Request is routed to queryREST.Connect() for the new query service\\n3. handleQuery() parses and prepares the request\\n4. handlePreparedQuery() invokes service.QueryData()\\n5. ServiceImpl.queryData() routes based on expression vs datasource queries\\n6. For datasources: handleQuerySingleDatasource() builds backend.QueryDataRequest\\n7. Single-tenant: pluginClient.QueryData() \u2192 plugin backend execution\\n8. Multi-tenant: ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest() \u2192 query-service client \u2192 aggregator plugin query handler\\n9. Plugin middleware stack processes the request\\n10. Plugin backend executes QueryData and returns QueryDataResponse\\n11. Response is wrapped in v0alpha1.QueryDataResponse with proper HTTP status codes\\n12. Responder serializes and sends the response\\n\\nFor expression queries, the path diverges to TransformData() which internally uses the datasource clients to fetch data and apply transformations.\"\n}\n",

The getDSQueryEndpoint() handler detects feature flags to either route to the legacy path or the new query service API.\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go** - Kubernetes-style REST API layer implementing the K8s API server pattern. The queryREST struct implements the Connect() method which returns an HTTP handler that processes POST requests to execute queries. This is the primary entry point for the new query service.\\n\\n## 2. Query Request Handler and Dispatch\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go** - The handleQuery() function processes incoming QueryDataRequest objects, extracts headers, and routes to the appropriate handler. The prepareQuery() function normalizes datasource references and builds the MetricRequest used by the legacy query service. The handlePreparedQuery() function invokes the legacy query service.\\n\\n**pkg/services/query/query.go** - The ServiceImpl implements the core query execution logic. Key methods:\\n- queryData() - Routes queries based on whether they contain expressions or target single/multiple datasources\\n- handleQuerySingleDatasource() - For single datasource queries, creates a backend.QueryDataRequest and dispatches to either the legacy plugin client (single-tenant) or the query-service client (multi-tenant) via ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest()\\n- handleExpressions() - For expression queries, delegates to the expression service's TransformData()\\n- executeConcurrentQueries() - Handles multiple datasource queries concurrently and aggregates responses\\n\\n## 3. Plugin Backend Query Dispatch\\n\\n**pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go** - The Service.QueryData() method looks up the plugin from the registry and invokes its QueryData handler. It handles error wrapping, request cancellation, and ensures frame RefIDs are set from response RefIDs.\\n\\n**pkg/plugins/backendplugin/coreplugin/core_plugin.go** - Core plugin implementation that wraps backend plugin handlers and invokes them with proper Grafana config context.\\n\\n**pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/query.go** - The QueryDataHandler() processes query requests in the aggregator layer (for multi-tenant deployments). It validates datasource references, obtains plugin context, and dispatches to the plugin client.\\n\\n**pkg/aggregator/apiserver/plugin/handler.go** - The PluginHandler routes requests to appropriate service handlers based on the aggregation service specification. For QueryServiceType, it routes to the QueryDataHandler().\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/datasource/sub_query.go** - Sub-resource query handler for direct datasource querying. The Connect() method returns an HTTP handler that binds the QueryDataRequest, extracts queries, and dispatches to the plugin client.\\n\\n## 4. Expression and Query Transformation\\n\\n**pkg/expr/service.go** - The Service.TransformData() method processes expression pipelines. It executes the expression graph using the datasource clients to fetch data and transform it according to the expression configuration.\\n\\n**pkg/expr/query_convert.go** - ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest() converts backend.QueryDataRequest to the K8s-style data.QueryDataRequest format used by the query-service client. This enables single datasource queries in multi-tenant scenarios.\\n\\n## 5. Response Transformation and Marshaling\\n\\n**pkg/apis/datasource/v0alpha1/query.go** - Defines the QueryDataResponse wrapper type that embeds backend.QueryDataResponse and adds Kubernetes metadata. The GetResponseCode() helper function determines the appropriate HTTP status code based on response content.\\n\\n**pkg/registry/apis/query/query.go** - In the Connect() method's handler, the responder.Object() calls wrap the backend.QueryDataResponse in a query.QueryDataResponse before serialization. Error handling converts errors to appropriate error responses with proper status codes and error sources.\\n\\n**pkg/services/pluginsintegration/clientmiddleware/** - Middleware chain that wraps the plugin client:\\n- caching_middleware.go - Caches query results when applicable\\n- httpclient_middleware.go - Sets HTTP headers on plugin requests\\n- metrics_middleware.go - Records request metrics\\n- tracing_middleware.go - Adds distributed tracing spans\\n\\nThese middleware components intercept QueryData calls to add cross-cutting concerns before dispatching to the underlying plugin implementation.\\n\\n## Complete Query Path Chain\\n\\n1. HTTP request arrives at getDSQueryEndpoint() or queryREST.Connect()\\n2. Request is routed to queryREST.Connect() for the new query service\\n3. handleQuery() parses and prepares the request\\n4. handlePreparedQuery() invokes service.QueryData()\\n5. ServiceImpl.queryData() routes based on expression vs datasource queries\\n6. For datasources: handleQuerySingleDatasource() builds backend.QueryDataRequest\\n7. Single-tenant: pluginClient.QueryData() \u2192 plugin backend execution\\n8. Multi-tenant: ConvertBackendRequestToDataRequest() \u2192 query-service client \u2192 aggregator plugin query handler\\n9. Plugin middleware stack processes the request\\n10. Plugin backend executes QueryData and returns QueryDataResponse\\n11. Response is wrapped in v0alpha1.QueryDataResponse with proper HTTP status codes\\n12. Responder serializes and sends the response\\n\\nFor expression queries, the path diverges to TransformData() which internally uses the datasource clients to fetch data and apply transformations.\"\n}\n",
